<div id="review_2122460535" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2122460535" />
    <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries"><img alt="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557144778p2/15335689.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2122460535?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries">destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781250222039" href="/book/show/43263226-a-conjuring-of-light">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=otp">otp</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=owned-physical">owned-physical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=the-best-of-the-best">the-best-of-the-best</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2122460535" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12049318688830165343"><blockquote>#1 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1920506835' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Darker Shade of Magic</a> ★★★★★ <br/>#2 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1971365618' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Gathering of Shadows</a> ★★★★★<br/>#3 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2122460535' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Conjuring of Light</a> ★★★★★</blockquote> <br/>I’ve been putting off writing this review for a month, which is about the same length of time I put off finishing the book itself, because I simply have not been prepared to say goodbye to this trilogy. Reading these three books has been one of the most emotional, anxiety-inducing, and genuinely <b>magical</b> experiences of my entire life. I have so much to say, with no idea how to express any of it.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“Love </b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText12049318688830165343" style="display:none"><blockquote>#1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1920506835" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a> ★★★★★ <br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1971365618" rel="nofollow noopener">A Gathering of Shadows</a> ★★★★★<br />#3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2122460535" rel="nofollow noopener">A Conjuring of Light</a> ★★★★★</blockquote> <br />I’ve been putting off writing this review for a month, which is about the same length of time I put off finishing the book itself, because I simply have not been prepared to say goodbye to this trilogy. Reading these three books has been one of the most emotional, anxiety-inducing, and genuinely <b>magical</b> experiences of my entire life. I have so much to say, with no idea how to express any of it.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“Love and loss,” he said, “are like a ship and the sea. They rise together. The more we love, the more we have to lose. But the only way to avoid loss is to avoid love. And what a sad world that would be.”</b>
</blockquote><br />I can safely say that I have never loved every character in a series the way I do with this one. I mourned every loss, laughed and cried tears of joy over each close call, every triumph, every kiss and reunion. The thing about this trilogy is that there are certain evils which must be faced and conquered, but what really <i>stays</i> with you is the build-up of these characters and their relationships with one another. I can’t even choose a favorite, because I love them all so much, in such different ways.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“Scars are not shameful, not unless you let them be. If you do not wear them, they will wear you.”</b>
</blockquote><br />In typical Schwab fashion, though, the action scenes are downright <i>glorious.</i> I love that, no matter how many moving pieces are in a battle, I never struggle to keep up with exactly what is happening, because her writing is so immersive that it transports you right into the center of the fight. You never know quite what twist or slight of hand to expect next.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b> “What are we drinking to?”<br />“The living,” said Rhy.<br />“The dead,” said Alucard and Lila at the same time.<br />“We’re being thorough,” added Rhy.</b>
</blockquote><br />Of course, it’s not all war and heartache; there are always these gorgeous moments woven in of bonding, of bickering and playful banter. I don’t think I’ve ever laughed so much in so many moments of sheer and utter anxiety, but that’s this series in a nutshell—especially the second and third installments. I actually joked recently that I’m so happy there is going to be a spin-off series, but at the same time, I need ample room to recover before putting my heart through the misery of another book with these characters scaring me half to death and breaking my heart every other chapter.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b> “Death comes for us all. I would simply have mine mean something.”</b>
</blockquote><br />I don’t know what else to say at this point. I wanted this review to be eloquent and thorough, but when I think back on this story, I am immediately pulled into such reminiscence for the <i>feelings</i> it drew out of me that I have a hard time viewing it subjectively and squaring it off into little, easy to describe compartments.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“<i>Anoshe</i> was a word for strangers in the street, and lovers between meetings, for parents and children, friends and family. It softened the blow of leaving. Eased the strain of parting. A careful nod to the certainty of today, the mystery of tomorrow. When a friend left, with little chance of seeing home, they said <i>anoshe</i>. When a loved one was dying, they said <i>anoshe</i>. When corpses were burned, bodies given back to the earth and souls to the stream, those left grieving said <i>anoshe</i>.<br /><br /><i>Anoshe</i> brought solace. And hope. And the strength to let go.”</b>
</blockquote><br />A month after completing it, I feel comfortable in now saying that this is <b>the single greatest series I have ever read in my life,</b> and Victoria Schwab has solidified a permanent place in my heart. I will buy anything and everything she writes in the future, and I will doubtlessly reread this trilogy over and over again. The writing is so flawless, and frankly, you could just tattoo this whole damn trilogy onto my body if there was enough room, and I’d be just fine with that, thank you.<br /><br />You can find this review and more on my <a href="https://howlinglibraries.com/2018/08/03/a-conjuring-of-light/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>, or you can follow me on <a href="https://twitter.com/howlinglibrary" rel="nofollow noopener">twitter</a>, <a href="https://instagram.com/howlinglibraries" rel="nofollow noopener">bookstagram</a>, or <a href="https://facebook.com/howlinglibraries" rel="nofollow noopener">facebook</a>!<br /><br />---<br /><br />Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/51076954-terry-tipton" rel="nofollow noopener">Terry</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7772979-jue" rel="nofollow noopener">Julie</a>! ♥♥♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="12049318688830165343" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" href="/user/show/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin">Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1918024587" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17136413418143590070"><b>LORD HAVE MERCY! THIS BOOK!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488751800i/22150802.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488751800ra/22150803.gif' alt=' ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was so afraid to go into it because I just knew everyone was going to die and that would be it, THEN END! Yes, people died. Yes, I let out some tears at parts. Yes, it was amaze balls. Yes, there was a lot of blood and violence. Yes, there was evil and magic and good. YES! YES! YES! <br/><br/>I love Rhy, Kell, Lila and Alucard so much. I even started to love ole Holland. There are other side people too. ❤<br/><br/>There is so much stuff going on. It starts right out of the gate and just</span>
  <span id="freeText17136413418143590070" style="display:none"><b>LORD HAVE MERCY! THIS BOOK!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488751800i/22150802.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488751800ra/22150803.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was so afraid to go into it because I just knew everyone was going to die and that would be it, THEN END! Yes, people died. Yes, I let out some tears at parts. Yes, it was amaze balls. Yes, there was a lot of blood and violence. Yes, there was evil and magic and good. YES! YES! YES! <br><br>I love Rhy, Kell, Lila and Alucard so much. I even started to love ole Holland. There are other side people too. ❤<br><br>There is so much stuff going on. It starts right out of the gate and just doesn't really stop. Maybe a break here and there but not too much. I think this was a perfect ending to this trilogy. <br><br>And I love that Lila is a bad@ssed woman in the book! I love when author's add a woman that can kick arse and take names. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Tell you what, " said the first attacker. "If you beg, we'll make it quick."<br><br>Lila's blood sang the way it always did before a fight, clear and bright and hungry. "And why," she said, "would I want to rush your deaths?"<br><br>"Cocky bitch," growled the second. "I'm gonna fu--"<br><br>Her knife hissed through the air and embedded itself in his throat. Blood spilled down his front as he clawed at his neck and toppled forward, and she made it under the next man's guard before the body hit the ground, driving her serrated blade up through his chin before the first blow caught her, a fist to the jaw. <br><br>She went down hard, spitting blood into the street. <br><br>Heat coursed through her limbs as a hand grabbed her by the hair and hauled her to her feed, a knife under her chin. <br><br>"Any last words?" asked the man with the rotting teeth. <br><br>Lila held up her hands, as if in surrender, before flashing a vicious smile. <br><br>"Tyger, Tyger," she said, and the fire roared to life.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>If you haven't read this trilogy and have been wanting to, I suggest you get on it because it's freaking awesome! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488752647i/22150864._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Anoshe.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2017/03/a-conjuring-of-light-by-ve-schwab.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9990462375440869206"><b>Patient Name:</b> Pragya Maresh Bard<br/><b>Status:</b> DEAD<br/><b>Cause of death:</b> Unknown; possible sources: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7168230.V_E__Schwab' title='V.E. Schwab' rel='nofollow noopener'>V.E. Schwab</a><br/><b>Symptoms:</b> Screaming; thrashing; crying profusely; repeatedly muttering <i>lila bard</i> <br/><b>Diagnosis: </b>WHAT THE FUCK I AM DEAD HOLY SHIT<br/><br/><s>SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT S</s></span>
  <span id="freeText9990462375440869206" style="display:none"><b>Patient Name:</b> Pragya Maresh Bard<br><b>Status:</b> DEAD<br><b>Cause of death:</b> Unknown; possible sources: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7168230.V_E__Schwab" title="V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">V.E. Schwab</a><br><b>Symptoms:</b> Screaming; thrashing; crying profusely; repeatedly muttering <i>lila bard</i> <br><b>Diagnosis: </b>WHAT THE FUCK I AM DEAD HOLY SHIT<br><br><s>SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT SANCT</s> <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488080548i/22079027.png" width="600" height="3" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>WARNING: <b>SPOILERS AHEAD</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488080548i/22079027.png" width="600" height="3" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><br><u><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=h_m-BjrxmgI" rel="nofollow noopener">De<b>lila</b>h</a> Bard</u>:<br><br><i>He said she was mad and stubborn and no use to us dead</i> - an accurate summary of lila bard by tieren, head priest and knower of things<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You think this is a bad idea,” he said. It wasn’t a question. But it sparked something in Lila, rekindled the fire in her eyes and ignited a grin. <br>“Without a doubt.”<br>“Then why are you smiling?”<br>“Because,” she said, “bad ideas are my favorite kind.”</blockquote>
</b><br>It’s no secret (if you know me at all) that I identify as <b>Lila Trash™</b>, and @allthehaters, here's a list of reasons why LILA BARD IS AWESOME AND YOU'RE WRONG:<blockquote>1. SHE SINGLE HANDEDLY RESCUED KELL FROM A PARALLEL UNIVERSE FROM A CAGE PROTECTED BY THE SHARPEST KNIGHT IN WHITE LONDON<br>2. <b>She's fucking badass</b>.<br>3. She's Lila Bard and she doesn't give a damn.</blockquote>My friend (who <i>hated</i> Lila) said she wasn't <i>as annoying</i> in this book. And I suppose, in a sense it's true - she went through a hell lot of character development. <b>She hated goodbyes, but she said them. She hated caring, but she cared anyway. She wanted to run, but she stayed anyway.</b> These subtle changes were far more powerful than any words could be. <br><br><br><br>If book #1 was Kell and book #2 was Lila, this was <b>Holland</b>. Holland, who <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7168230.V_E__Schwab" title="V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">V.E. Schwab</a> ships with sadness. Holland, who <b>lost everything but still fought for his world.</b> Holland, who broke my heart because FUCK NOBODY DESERVES SO MUCH PAIN.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>The bodies piled. Athos watched. Astrid grinned. Holland’s hand moved on its puppet string. And his mind screamed until it finally lost its voice.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488080548i/22079027.png" width="600" height="3" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><b><br> - Kell x Lila: </b>They kiss so much?? Honestly I should have kept count of how many times they kiss because they’re rushing off to danger every two seconds and just kiss before all the time<i> just for luck</i> you know<br> - also LILA ALMOST DIED and kell breaks apart and jfc he carries her back and hugs her and <b>MY HEART</b><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488080548i/22079027.png" width="600" height="3" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><br><b> - Rhylucard:</b> I SHIP THEM SO MUCH. SO DAMN MUCH. <br> - I swear, 75% of my highlights from this book are rhylucard moments because they're so precious honestly<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Luc?” rasped Rhy.<br>“I’m here,” answered Alucard. “I’m here. Stay with me.”<br>He tried to speak, but his heart slammed against his ribs as if trying to break through.<br>It redoubled, then faltered.</b>
</blockquote> - He woke up and called him luc my heart is over he was dying and what he thought of what said was luc jfc<br><blockquote>
  <b>Alucard clutched his lover’s hand.</b>
</blockquote> - HE CALLED HIM HIS LOVER I AM DEAD I AM DYING<br> - THE WORLD WENT TO HELL AND YOU KNOW WHAT ALUCARD’S REACTION WAS: <br><blockquote>
  <b>All that mattered - all that would ever matter - was this.<br>Rhy was alive.</b>
</blockquote> - I mean, how can you <i>not</i> cry reading that?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488080548i/22079027.png" width="600" height="3" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><br><b>Also can we talk about Kell on Rhylucard &amp; Alucard walking in on Kell and Lila because it's the best thing ever: </b> <br><br> - I love Protective Kell™ so much <br><b>
  <blockquote>“I told you to keep him safe, not cuddle”</blockquote>
</b><br><br> - also this:<br><b>
  <blockquote>“Kell,” she said, the word something between a whisper and a gasp. <br>And then the door burst open. <br>Alucard stood in the doorway, soaking wet, as if he’d just been dumped in the sea, or the sea had been dumbed over him. <i><br>“Stop fucking with the ship.”</i>
</blockquote>
</b><br> - I have never laughed so much in my life<br><br><br><br>This book is a monster. Actually - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7168230.V_E__Schwab" title="V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">V.E. Schwab</a> is a monster. A beautiful cold hearted monster who will stop at nothing less than my death. Well? There you have it. <u>A GODAMM PERFECT ENDING.</u><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>This is why I run. Because caring was a thing with claws. It sank them in, and didn’t let go. Caring hurt more than a knife to the leg, motor then anything that bled or broke and healed again. Caring didn’t break you clean. It was a bone that didn’t set, a cut that wouldn’t close. </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488080548i/22079027.png" width="600" height="3" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>VERDICT: <b>VICTORIA SCHWAB HAS SHATTERED ME AND I DON'T KNOW IF I'LL EVER BE FINE. WHAT I <i>DO</i> KNOW IS THAT EVERYBODY ON THIS PLANET NEEDS THIS TRILOGY IN THERE LIFE.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488080548i/22079027.png" width="600" height="3" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <u>pre-review(<i>s</i>) because I'm trash lmao</u>
</blockquote><br><br><u>update:</u> IT'S HERE OH MY GOD I'M SCARED TO ACTUALLY READ IT WTF<br><br><b>another update because I CAN'T CONTAIN MY EXCITEMENT WHAT IS THIS LIFE I NEED THIS BUT I CAN'T READ IT will probably skip school and read it the second it comes out because yes I'm <i>Trash</i> honestly I've never wanted anything in my life so much?? </b><br><br>ALSO I HEARD THERE'S DEATH I WILL SUE IF THERE'S DEATH<br><br>(messages from me to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/49148508" rel="nofollow noopener">may</a> and honestly i'm mad because nobody's as excited for this as I am HELLO IT'LL BE THE END OF AN ERA) (also i feel like it's been a lot of time since I said this but <b>I LOVE LILA BARD</b> just an update)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487247153i/21991032.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487247346i/21991074.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487247657i/21991121.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487247346i/21991075._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487247346i/21991076._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Do you know what I just realised? (yes this is an update because I thought I was ready, guess what I'M NOT)<br></b><br>This book releases in <u>18 days.</u><br>Which is to say, <u>432 hours.<br>259200 minutes.</u><br><br><b>15552000 seconds till we get more Kell and Lila and Alucard and Rhy.</b><br><br><s>I know it's not accurate. Fight me.</s></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12827670710704212235">Updated 9/11/17:<br/>I will be crying for the next 75 years. This was perfection. It was such a good conclusion.<br/><br/>▪️▪️▪️<br/>UMMMMM so I finished A Gathering of Shadows and placed an order for this book within 10 minutes. <div id="review_1609936465" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1609936465" />
    <a title="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud"><img alt="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517124730p2/14717996.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1609936465?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud">Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》</a>
      </span>

          marked it as never-ever-ever




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1609936465" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10177336585730748210">DNF 39%<br/><br/>Disclaimer: It's not the book, it might just be me! <br/><br/>Here is the thing, i thoroughly enjoyed Darker Shades of Magic and Gathering of Shadows! However, having to wait an entire year has ruined this series for me. I no longer care about the plot or give any shits about what happens to these characters. I've simply moved on, it seems. This is precisely why i loath starting unfinished series. I am sure it's not a bad book but since i didn't like however much i read, i can't rate it any higher.</span>
  <span id="freeText10177336585730748210" style="display:none">DNF 39%<br /><br />Disclaimer: It's not the book, it might just be me! <br /><br />Here is the thing, i thoroughly enjoyed Darker Shades of Magic and Gathering of Shadows! However, having to wait an entire year has ruined this series for me. I no longer care about the plot or give any shits about what happens to these characters. I've simply moved on, it seems. This is precisely why i loath starting unfinished series. I am sure it's not a bad book but since i didn't like however much i read, i can't rate it any higher. <br /><br />(based on what i read)<br /><br />There is no character development whatsoever. <br />AH, it bothers me so much. (except Holland)<br />Lila, let's talk about her first. What is the matter with her? I didn't mind her recklessness in the first book, quite enjoyed it actually. In the second book, however, it was getting a little too ridiculous. i also saw others complaining about it as well, i still decided to overlook it. STUPID ME! This one was just way over the top! This has got to stop. It was just annoying and unrealistic. I couldn't read this bullshit any longer let alone actually take it seriously. <br /><br />Kell. My precious baby Kell. Oh, how i loved you for years, Kell! You people probably don't have any idea how much I appreciated a character like Kell, who isn't a cliched alpha male crap. (that seems to be the most recent trend in YA *rolls eyes*) His loneliness, him wanting to just belong somewhere got me, man! He seemed totally out of character in this last book. He was whiny and boring AF. Not a great combination, I must say. <br /><br />I can't stand them as a couple!! They didn't have to be romanticly involved. It felt forced. I've always had an extremely hard time imagining Lila being in a relationship with anyone. IT'S MANON BLACKBEAK ALL OVER AGAIN!!! I'm disgusted and disappointed. <br /><br />Then there are Rhy and Alucard, who i absolutely, 100% do not give a shit about. <br /><br />I wanted to keep reading this for Holland.. maybe one day I'll finish it. Just for him.</span>

<div id="review_1927314601" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1927314601" />
    <a title="Anne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1720620-anne"><img alt="Anne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415374035p2/1720620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1927314601?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne" href="/user/show/1720620-anne">Anne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=magic-stuff">magic-stuff</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1927314601" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10576564179982474437"><i>
  <b>Ehhhhhh.</b>
</i><br/>I finished this one a while back, but I just couldn't decide how I felt about it.<br/>I mean, it was <i>ok</i>. Nothing was horribly wrong, and I certainly didn't feel pissed off when I closed the book. It just left me with this vaguely <i>meh</i> feeling.<br/>Like...<i>why did I read all of this?</i><br/>This was, at 624 pages, a HUGE book. <--for me!<br/>I know some of you read massive tomes every night before bed, but I usually snack on comic books or fluffy romance novels, so when these bigguns don't deliver I feel a ta</span>
  <span id="freeText10576564179982474437" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Ehhhhhh.</b>
</i><br>I finished this one a while back, but I just couldn't decide how I felt about it.<br>I mean, it was <i>ok</i>. Nothing was horribly wrong, and I certainly didn't feel pissed off when I closed the book. It just left me with this vaguely <i>meh</i> feeling.<br>Like...<i>why did I read all of this?</i><br>This was, at 624 pages, a HUGE book. &lt;--for me!<br>I know some of you read massive tomes every night before bed, but I usually snack on comic books or fluffy romance novels, so when these bigguns don't deliver I feel a tad disappointed.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494432814ra/22714268.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I'm not actually saying it <i>didn't deliver</i>, because look at all the bjillion 5 star reviews! Apparently, I'm one of the few people on the planet that had a lukewarm reaction to <b>A Conjuring of Light</b>, so please don't take this review as a slam on the book. It's a solid finish to the trilogy, there are no dangling threads left out there, and I was (for the most part) satisfied by the way it wrapped up.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494435805ra/22714571.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Schwab is a fantastic storyteller, and since she's managed to write my oldest son's favorite story <i>ever</i> <b>--&gt; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/729148703" rel="nofollow noopener">Vicious</a></b>, I'm afraid if I say anything less than glowing I'll have to sleep with one eye open. <br><i>You never know with kids these days...</i><br>*ducks*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494435805ra/22714572.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Still, I did have a few issues. I'll tag the ones that are possible spoilers...<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>The two spoilery things I wasn't crazy about were Holland's ending, and Kells magic pains.<br>First, Holland. I guess not everyone gets a happy ending, but <i>man</i>! That dude never got to have a good day in his LIFE! Everyone he ever knew was HORRIBLE to him, then he was tortured for years by those psycho twins, and after sacrificing his life once already...everyone in Red London still hates his guts. It was bad enough that the poor guy ended up slinking off to his own dimension to die (and maybe rejuvenate his London? Vague, much?), but why in the hell didn't Kell explain to everyone that Holland had been unable to control his actions while the Dane twins were alive. I mean, that would have gone a long way toward Lila forgiving him for that dude's death. And, yes, he was responsible for the evil dude escaping Black London, but give me a fucking break! The guy was half dead, stranded in a different dimension (after Kell killed him, btw!), and he thought letting that <i>thing</i> possess him might save his people. Can we not cut the poor fella any slack?<br>To me, it felt like he was just the whipping boy so that there could be a <i>tragic</i> hero...who wasn't Kell.<br>Which brings us to Kell and his ouchie magic.<br>Why? Why does it now hurt every time he does magic? I mean, I know <i>why</i>...I read it! But it just seemed tacked on so that no one could accuse Schwab of going easy on her main character. So, yeah, he lives. But it hurts when he does magic now. <br>Whatever. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>I guess the other thing I wasn't crazy about was Lila and Kell's relationship. It never felt genuine or even really romantic. I don't know why, but they just seemed like a very dull couple. And I think Schwab can write depth to her romantic attachments because Rhy and Alucard had depth.<br><br><i>P.S. This has <b>nothing</b> to do with the story, but I could not for the life of me stop thinking:</i><b> Alucard is Dracula spelled backward!</b><br><i>My kids used to LOVE <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0472219/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Batman vs. Dracula</a> movie and there was this one scene in it that kept running through my mind during this entire book...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494437365i/22714733.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494437365i/22714734._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Dun, dun, duuun! <i>*gasp!*</i></b><br><br>Anyway. <br>I guess the rest of it was fine. There was some great stand out moments that I really enjoyed, and I think anyone who has read the first 2 books should be satisfied with this last installment. Overall though, I can't say I this would be a series/trilogy that I'd want to reread.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10576564179982474437" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=signed">signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=urban">urban</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1922011027" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13151362977173125104"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1525814492i/25506830._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Darker Shade of Magic</a> ★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1572707686' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Gathering of Shadows</a> ★★★<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love and loss,” he said, “are like a ship and the sea. They rise together. The more we love, the more we have to lose. But the only way to avoid loss is to avoid love. And what a sad world that would be.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I have read one book in this series every year for the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/163712-booktubesff-awards' rel='nofollow noopener'>BooktubeSFF Awards</a>. And every year I enjoy what I’m reading, I close the book pretty pleased, and then I sit down to write my review and start thinking about how these</span>
  <span id="freeText13151362977173125104" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1525814492i/25506830._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a> ★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1572707686" rel="nofollow noopener">A Gathering of Shadows</a> ★★★<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love and loss,” he said, “are like a ship and the sea. They rise together. The more we love, the more we have to lose. But the only way to avoid loss is to avoid love. And what a sad world that would be.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I have read one book in this series every year for the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/163712-booktubesff-awards" rel="nofollow noopener">BooktubeSFF Awards</a>. And every year I enjoy what I’m reading, I close the book pretty pleased, and then I sit down to write my review and start thinking about how these are such big books with so little happening. And I know they are character driven. One of my favorite books of all time is the most character driven thing out there, but for some reason I just don’t love this series like everyone else does. <br><br><i>A Conjuring of Light</i> is the third and final novel in this trilogy that surround four different parallel Londons:<br>➽ <b>Grey London</b> - is like our real world's London, with no magic. Delilah Bard is from this London.<br>➽ <b>Red London</b> - is the home of the main protagonist, Kell, where he and his royal family rule. There is an abundance of magic in this London, most coming from a red river which lights up the whole city.<br>➽ <b>White London</b> - is a city in war with itself. It was ruled by evil twins, but now has a new king. Everyone in this London tries to fight for magic and power within this corrupt city.<br>➽ <b>Black London</b> - and is still basically a mystery. It is essentially a lost city, since regular people cannot travel between worlds.<br><br>And after the brutal cliffhanger ending that was <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1572707686" rel="nofollow noopener">A Gathering of Shadows</a>, <i>A Conjuring of Light</i> picks right back up after the events! And without saying anything too spoilery, since this is the concluding novel and all, our main character, Kell Maresh, and his home, Red London, are in serious danger. But with the help of a ruthless thief/assassin, Lila Bard, a swoon-worthy pirate, Alucard Emery, the best prince to have ever lived, Rhy Maresh, and a very morally grey Antari, Holland Vosijk, they are trying to save everything they’ve ever known and loved. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Life isn't made of choices, it's made of trades. Some are good, some are bad, but they all have a cost.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And even the idea of four different color coded Londons, with a handful of magical people who can travel between them, is so damn genius that I don’t even have words for it. Also, V.E. Schwab is such a talented writer. The way she echoes phrases from different books, or even sentences from previous chapters, is so powerful and is able to evoke all the emotions from me. She truly can weave and craft paragraphs together so expertly and I’m constantly impressed with her writing. <br><br>I just feel like not a lot happens in her books. Like, a few big, key, important things happen without question, and storylines get completed, but I just feel like it is such a longwinded journey to get there. And these books are so easily consumable that you don’t really realize until after you’ve closed the book. I mean, at least for me and my personal reading experiences. Seriously, go back and look at my other two reviews; I say the same thing. Also, the big bad villain just fell so very short for me. The magic started off so dang well, but the villain really ended up feeling lackluster to me.<br><br>But my biggest complaint about the other two installments in this series is that they don’t read or feel adult to me. But you know what <i>A Conjuring of Light</i> reads and feels like? Adult, without question. Also, just a little caveat, if an author says their work is in a certain age bracket/genre, then it is. I am just saying <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459616912" rel="nofollow noopener">A Darker Shade of Magic</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1572707686" rel="nofollow noopener">A Gathering of Shadows</a> don’t feel or read like adult fantasy to me, but I’m not saying they aren’t. But <i>ACOL</i> did give me those brutal moments that made me go “okay, this isn’t YA” quite a lot. <br><br>Also, <b>trigger and content warnings</b> for abuse, torture, abduction, slavery, captivity, talk of suicide, violence, gore, heavy blood depiction, abandonment, and depiction of grief and PTSD. Oh and I guess sexual content, too, but nothing too graphic. (Also, hello, perverted Melanie here to report that that sex scene was 11/10 and was so smooth and sexy and I actually loved it!) <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I have never known what to make of you. Not since the day we met. And it terrifies me. You terrify me. And the idea of you walking away again, vanishing from my life, that terrifies me most of all.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But my biggest love for this series is Rhy Maresh, who has completely and without question stole my heart. He is easily my favorite character in this series. My beautiful, pure, cinnamon roll, unbreakable boy. I stan one man from this series, and it’s him. And he deserves everything good in the universe. <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1527120358i/25587449.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Breathtaking art <a href="https://www.tumblr.com/reblog/166414541841/euYKg7RZ?redirect_to=%2Fsearch%2Fa%2Bdarker%2Bshade%2Bof%2Bmagic%2Fpost_page%2F9" rel="nofollow noopener"> meliescribbles</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We don't choose what we are, but we choose what we do.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Overall, take this review with a large grain of salt. I am for sure in the minority with not loving these books as much as everyone else. And even though this isn’t my favorite series, I think Victoria is incredibly talented and I can’t wait to see what she does next. And I truly think that these books get better and better, with <i>A Conjuring of Light</i> being my favorite in the series, and the last couple chapters of this book had me smiling from ear to ear in pure happiness. And I ultimately do feel really fulfilled and happy with the ending. Plus, I’m very interested (especially after gushing with my friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7772979-jue" rel="nofollow noopener">Julie</a>) with reading the graphic novel series set around a character from this world. Also, I have the highest of hopes for the spinoff that Victoria is working on. I just hope I fall completely head over heels in love, instead of only just enjoying. <br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a><br><br>Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/14843185.Julie_Zantopoulos" rel="nofollow by:</b><br>🌑 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/30749549-samantha" rel="nofollow noopener">Samantha</a> from <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCUfP0El1vakyfkkXbyJwy0Q" rel="nofollow <div id="review_1999876505" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1999876505" />
    <a title="Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen"><img alt="Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560356189p2/47627265.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1999876505?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)" href="/user/show/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen">Kaylin (The Re-Read Queen)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kaylin by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/61971658-frankie-lovely">Frankie Lovely</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=recommended-to-me">recommended-to-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=memorable-male-characters">memorable-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=almost-great">almost-great</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1999876505" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11584822438818633552"><b>4.25 Stars<br/><br/>Overview: </b><br/><br/><i>
  <blockquote>“Anoshe was a word for strangers in the street, and lovers between meetings, for parents and children, friends and family. It softened the blow of leaving.” </blockquote>
</i><br/><br/>Okay, I know my rating is picky and oddly specific, but it’s true. I enjoyed this more than AGOS (making it my favorite of the series) but it's still <i>just</i> shy of 5 stars. <br/><br/>In fact, that's what I rated it in a blind-emotional fury immediately after I finished. Because there was a lot I <i>loved.</i> ...But also some stuff I di</span>
  <span id="freeText11584822438818633552" style="display:none"><b>4.25 Stars<br /><br />Overview: </b><br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“Anoshe was a word for strangers in the street, and lovers between meetings, for parents and children, friends and family. It softened the blow of leaving.” </blockquote>
</i><br /><br />Okay, I know my rating is picky and oddly specific, but it’s true. I enjoyed this more than AGOS (making it my favorite of the series) but it's still <i>just</i> shy of 5 stars. <br /><br />In fact, that's what I rated it in a blind-emotional fury immediately after I finished. Because there was a lot I <i>loved.</i> ...But also some stuff I didn't. <br /><br />Another BR with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26402455-sana" rel="nofollow noopener">Sana</a>. (Even though she hated AGOS, smh.)<br /><br /><b>Pros:</b><br /><br />I need to read another Schwab book <i>like now.</i> This series was my first experience with her writing and I <i>love</i> it. She utilizes crisp sentences and sensory details so I can completely visualize the scene. She expertly lets the scene rise and fall and is a <i>master</i> at setting tone.<br /><br />Listen and let me tell you about my two new children: Rhy Maresh and Alucard Emery. I JUST REALLY LOVE BOTH OF THEM OKAY. <br /><br />Rhy especially has a <i>ton</i> of character development. I laughed with him at the beginning and here my heart broke for him. He has to step up so much and really come into his own as a leader and I just <i>love it.</i> <br /><br />Alucard and Kell bickering like old women is my new aesthetic. I could have honestly read a whole book about this, I swear. (But I also loved getting to see more of Luc’s backstory and taking him more seriously)<br /><br />The ending works very well. No spoilers, but everyone ends up in believable places and there’s certainly ramifications. <br /><br />Speaking of which, the villain here is kind of <i>awesome.</i> Not quite the direction I was expecting for this series, but it works very well and I loved getting inside his head.<br /><br />There are certain scenes the whole series seemed to be building towards and they are <i>tense.</i> Very well done and some of these really blew my mind. <br /><br />Yes, hello it is I. Still loving Holland and just silently weeping in the background. Just such a dynamic character with such a strong presence on the page. <br /><br /><b>Cons:</b><br /><br />At almost 700 pages, this is a little long. Places seemed overstuffed while others seemed off-topic, and there just some major pacing issues. The first 100 pages or so take off right after the explosive ending of AGOS, but then everything veers one direction and then another and sort of clambers together by the ending. <br /><br />I really liked a lot of these elements, but couldn’t help by feel they were a little random? This floating market idea was super cool and I loved the way it played out, but it literally <i>came out of nowhere.</i><br /><br />There were several characters who were expanded upon here—the king, queen, visitors from neighboring cities and others. While I really enjoyed their perspectives and how they impacted the story, it felt a little out of place to just <i>now</i> learn about these characters. I wish a lot of this started in the second book. <br /><br />Listen: Lila is a fun character, but she has no development. <br /><br />She seems almost exactly the same here as she did at the beginning of ADSOM. She definitely is fun, and I love how capable she is. But at some point the narrative switched to <i>continually</i> telling me what a bad-ass she is. She felt ridiculously <i>over-powered.</i> Why did the second book include a whole plot about magic having consequences and Kell warning her about her recklessness if nothing comes of it???<br /><br /><b>In Conclusion:</b><br /><br /><i>Anoshe </i><br /><br /><br />-----------------------------<br /><br />I'm here for Rhy and Luc. ❤️❤️<br /><br />(And maybe even Kell) <br /><br />(Everyone but Lila, probably)</span>
  <a data-text-id="11584822438818633552" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <td colspan="2">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1475502382" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer105844981161835787"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Anoshe was a word for strangers in the street, and lovers between meetings, for parents and children, friends and family. It softened the blow of leaving. Eased the strain of parting. A careful nod to the certainty of today, the mystery of tomorrow. When a friend left, with little chance of seeing home, they said anoshe. When a loved one was dying, they said anoshe. When corpses were burned, bodies given back to the earth and souls to the stream, those left grieving said anoshe. <br/>Anoshe b</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText105844981161835787" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Anoshe was a word for strangers in the street, and lovers between meetings, for parents and children, friends and family. It softened the blow of leaving. Eased the strain of parting. A careful nod to the certainty of today, the mystery of tomorrow. When a friend left, with little chance of seeing home, they said anoshe. When a loved one was dying, they said anoshe. When corpses were burned, bodies given back to the earth and souls to the stream, those left grieving said anoshe. <br>Anoshe brought solace. And hope. And the strength to let go.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>me: *slams fist on table* time to write acol review<br>inner me: you can't write a serious one even if they paid you<br>inner me: you're going to babble and yell incoherently<br>inner me: it would be full of cringe<br>inner me: and you will also cry<br>me: *slams two fists on table* THATS THE PLAN<br><br>I HONESTLY DONT KNOW WHERE TO START. SO MANY FEELINGS.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29939230.A_Conjuring_of_Light__Shades_of_Magic___3_" title="A Conjuring of Light (Shades of Magic, #3) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">acol</a> is a beautiful conclusion of one of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/122142-shades-of-magic" rel="nofollow noopener">my most favorite book series</a> and i spent 10 minutes crying because it's over. i can't easily let my favorite characters and one of my favorite worlds go.<br><br>i pulled an allnighter to read this book, i binge read it for 11 hours, had like 2 hours of sleep in two days, paced around my flat like a fucking zombie numb and empty after i finished it and I REGRET NOTHING. i loved this book so much!!! it's so intense, action-packed and glorious. i enjoyed the story and all characters interactions and i WISH it would've been longer (even tho its 600+ pages lmao)<br><br>this book made me cry so fucking much though. like, i don't cry easily and GODDAMN IT VICTORIA 	why. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29939230.A_Conjuring_of_Light__Shades_of_Magic___3_" title="A Conjuring of Light (Shades of Magic, #3) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">acol</a> made me feel so many things, it made me laugh, made me cry, made me so worried sometimes, i felt like dying. sometimes it was SO FUCKING CREEPY and sometimes it was so FLUFFY. also JEEZ there was no relaxing, something good happens and you're like 'oh phew' and then you turn the page AND SHIT HITS YOU IN THE FACE. pls give me a break????<br>i'm very sad that the story has ended but at the same time im very happy.<br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>A Conjuring of Light may mark the end of one adventure, but remember: when it comes to this world, new doors are always being made.</i></b><br>- Victoria Schwab</blockquote><br><br><b>!!!!!!!!!!<br>everything further contains spoilers which i won't mark as spoilers so PLEASE don't read it further if you haven't read the book yet<br>!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br><br><br>listen, i expected it to be cool, but it was way cooler??? but what's with this KILLING SPREE. remember when victoria was like oh this book is 35% death and i was like phew it doesnt sound so bad AND THEN THIS BOOK MURDERED LIKE EVERY SIDE CHARACTER I CARED ABOUT AND I WAS LIKE WHAT THE FUCK VICTORIA. i cried the hardest at calla's death, maxim's death, hastra's death (omg i cant even think abt it without tearing up??? he thought he was a bad guard and then he saved kell and,,,,send help why did my tiny son die he should've been a priest but then kell might've died WHY) AND HOLLAND'S DEATH (i knew holland would die and i knew he would die like he did (finally free and calm but JESUS. FUCKING. CHRIST. i didn't know i have so many tears in me).<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Death comes for us all,” said Holland evenly. “I would simply have mine mean something.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>about holland though. for me he was the highlight of this book. i didn't like him in the first book and then <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20764879.A_Gathering_of_Shadows__Shades_of_Magic___2_" title="A Gathering of Shadows (Shades of Magic, #2) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">agos</a> happened and i softened to him BUT IN THIS FUCKING BOOK HE JUST BROKE MY HEART SO MANY TIMES MY SOFT SPOT FOR HIM IS THE SIZE OF OUR UNIVERSE. he got a redemption arc and this redemption arc is 9138483/10, his backstory made me cry so many times (like, his brother tried to kill him when he was a little boy???? a girl he loved and was happy with tried to kill him?? his best friend was killed and he couldn't save him??? he was tortured and captured and he couldn't do anything about it but just count his kills (i will never stop crying that he did it) and suffer??? and then it happened again after he just got free??? my poor tortured soN, i wanted to tuck him in the bed and cover him with all the blankets i have). i loved his interaction with kell so much and i loved holland so much and i can't convey my emotions about him in the text because DAMMIT he's totally the best character of this book and one of the best antagonists-but-not-really i've ever read about and can i have more characters like holland pretty please. i fucking started bawling when he trapped osaron and then i kept sobbing when he woke up and i couldn't stop weeping when he died because i knew it would happen and in a way it was a perfect ending for him (he died and his world lived and that is what he always desired and awknfaliefn im dead) but DAMN IT HURTS.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Lila met Holland’s gaze, expecting—maybe even hoping—to find that cold, implacable calm, perhaps tinged with disgust. Instead, she found shades of sadness, loss. And somehow, strength. The strength to go on. To try again. To trust.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>i loved INTERACTIONS in this book so much.<br><br>kell and rhy are forever my most favorite brother duo. they love and care about each other so much i would die for them.<br><br>rhy and alucard are two idiots in love and i hope they're forever happy. alucard's backstory is so horrible (i cant believe his brother survived but good people didnt wtf can he jump off a cliff thank u very much nobody needs him) and i'm so happy that rhy understood and forgave him and wjskfeafjsklfskl pls be happy.<br><br>kell and lila (!!!!!!!!!!!!!). i shipped them from the very beginning AND THEY FINALLY GOT TOGETHER AND THEY'RE SOOO CUUUUTEEE. i love kell and lila and their relationship and the fact that kell would rather shoot himsef in the head than trust her (jk). i love how they're different but they complete each other in their own way. i love that the series wasn't really focused on their romance, but it's still enough and it's beautiful and i want to cri. also kell is very efficient teacher isnt he.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Ned stared at her with open awe. “You’re like him.”<br>“No,”said Kell dryly, striding past him. “She’s one of a kind.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>kell and alucard gave me life with their bickering.<br><br>kell and holland!!!!!!!!!!! good shit right here!!!!!!!!!! kell cared about holland and i cried at this and i wish it was different between them, like, holland is so older brother material for kell and AAAAAAAAAAAAA. and holland, too, was pretty fond of kell here i think. and i want to weep again because it could've been so much more.<br><br>ALSO THE SQUAD aka kell, rhy, lila and alucard. omg how much i loved that scene when they drank together and their interactions overall AND I WISH THERE WERE MORE because damn this is the squad i can read hours about.<br><br>THE THREE ANTARI. one of the best things that happened in this book. i wanted this from the very beginning and YESSSS kell, lila and holland finally worked together AND HOLLAND WAS THE ANCHOR, THE CENTER and this is perfect??? <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Lila looked to Kell. “You didn’t teach me this one.”<br>His jaw was slack. “I …I didn’t know it.”<br>Holland gave them both a bland look. “Amazing,”he said dryly. “There are still things you haven’t learned.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>i loved all characters in this book, and thanks to victoria schwab for creating them and i cant believe i have to say good bye to them.<br><br>*cries externally*<br>*cries internally*<br>*cries eternally*<br><br>as i already said im pretty satisfied with the closure. but i'm not satisfied with complete lack of backstory for lila. like, kell's parents thing was at least acknowledged, holland got a decent backstory that i will never stop crying about, but lila got nothing. i wanted to know more about her from the very beginning of the series and we didn't even get glimpses into her past. (i also don't understand how she almost died when kell said 93289894 times in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22055262.A_Darker_Shade_of_Magic__Shades_of_Magic___1_" title="A Darker Shade of Magic (Shades of Magic, #1) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">adsom</a> that antari are almost invincible and it's really hard, almost impossible to kill them and then bam lila could've died if holland didn't heal her. i understand that her wound was fatal but idk). pretty much only issues i have with this book tho.<br><br>overall, for me this book was perfect. fast, intense and exciting. i wish it weren't the end.<br>pls hold me while im crying<br>12108392810293/10<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> It wasn’t a good-bye, not really. <br>What was the word for parting? <br>Anoshe.<br>That was it. <br>Until another day.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Anoshe.</b><br><br>~~~~~~~<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487672967i/22037656._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>did i finish this book or did this book finish me?<br><br>fyi i spent last two parts fucking bawling<br>my pillow is wet my nose is running my eyes are dry i feel empty and dead inside i need a hug<br><br>rtc hopefully<br><br>~~~~~~~<br><br>pre-reading:<br><s>*new updates are posted in the beginning</s><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487349023i/22003711._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>first of all, is this holland vs danes twins   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2670222549?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hamad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hamad" href="/user/show/54464244-hamad">Hamad</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781785652448" href="/book/show/32200595-a-conjuring-of-light">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54464244-hamad?shelf=good-covers">good-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54464244-hamad?shelf=2019-reads">2019-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54464244-hamad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54464244-hamad?shelf=gifts">gifts</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2670222549" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer174396503215102017"> <i>
  <b>“Life isn’t made of choices, it’s made of trades. Some are good, some are bad, but they all have a cost.” </b>
</i><br/><br/> * A Darker Shade Of Magic 🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/> * A Gathering of Shadows 🌟🌟🌟<br/> * A Conjuring of Light 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/><br/>🌟 This series has been on my TBR since before this book was even released and I kept procrastinating and the general rule in this situation is that I am always sleeping on a good book! I really enjoyed it that it deserved a 5 stars from me. This makes it the 4th book to get this rating out of 95 boo</span>
  <span id="freeText174396503215102017" style="display:none"> <i>
  <b>“Life isn’t made of choices, it’s made of trades. Some are good, some are bad, but they all have a cost.” </b>
</i><br><br> * A Darker Shade Of Magic 🌟🌟🌟🌟<br> * A Gathering of Shadows 🌟🌟🌟<br> * A Conjuring of Light 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br><br>🌟 This series has been on my TBR since before this book was even released and I kept procrastinating and the general rule in this situation is that I am always sleeping on a good book! I really enjoyed it that it deserved a 5 stars from me. This makes it the 4th book to get this rating out of 95 books I read this year and I will try to explain why.<br><br>🌟 After my mild disappointment with the second book which I thought was slow and suffered from middle book syndrome, I lowered my expectations significantly before starting this one as it was the largest, and I could not imagine reading 666 pages of slow pacing as in book 2.<br><br>🌟 What I love in Schwab’s writing is her small multiple chapters, this book almost had a 100 chapters (not kidding) and they were short which kept me attached to the story with the dreaded “just one more chapter”. This style became like Schwab’s specialty in writing as it could be found in most of her books.<br><br>🌟 Now small chapters alone are not a recipe for a good book, but add Schwab’s good writing and that would it make a very good recipe! There is something she does where she writes a kind of parallelism that I really really love and I don’t think I can give an example without spoilers so I will leave it for you to discover it in the book. There was the right mix of banter, sarcasm and serious writing at the right doses. I found many quotes that I really liked and if I highlighted them my book would have ended up half highlighted!<br><br> <i>
  <b>“What are we drinking to?”<br> “The living,” said Rhy.<br> “The dead,” said Alucard and Lila at the same time.<br> “We’re being thorough,” added Rhy. </b>
</i><br><br><br>🌟 The characters in this one developed immensely and then Schwab killed all of them! No, I am kidding but this was brutal and many characters do not make it so do not get attached to any of them! But I almost liked all of the characters whether they were primary or secondary ones!!<br><br>(Me, whenever I think about the characters in this book:)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1567360098i/28084908._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>🌟 Now the plot in this one was definitely better than the second book and it makes up for it because it felt like it was a bridge for all that happens in this one and a lot does happen specially at the beginning! There were a few questions that were left unanswered and a few things that felt like they were coincidences but in reality were very important for the story!<br><br>🌟 Summary: I loved this one, from the writing to the characters to the pacing and plot! It was an addicting book from start to end and although there were a few details that irked me, I am trying to ignore them for the majority of the book which was excellent and I will be continuing Schwab’s books in the future for sure!</span>
  <a data-text-id="174396503215102017" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Feels. <br/>hElp.</b><br/><a href='http://s1215.photobucket.com/user/morganaa13/media/Mood%20Gifs/rw1qzj8x3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/>This is hands down my <b>FAVORITE</b> book from the <i>Shades of Magic</i> trilogy! It's rare for me to be satisfied with a conclusion to a series as a lot of the times the spark gets lost along the way but not in ACOL's case.   <span id="freeText3640919401597003772" style="display:none"><i>"A myth without a voice is like a dandelion without a breath of wind. No way to spread the seeds."</i><br><b>Too. Much. Feels. <br>hElp.</b><br><a href="http://s1215.photobucket.com/user/morganaa13/media/Mood%20Gifs/rw1qzj8x3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494444303ra/22715518.gif" alt="hysterical crying photo rw1qzj8x3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>This is hands down my <b>FAVORITE</b> book from the <i>Shades of Magic</i> trilogy! It's rare for me to be satisfied with a conclusion to a series as a lot of the times the spark gets lost along the way but not in ACOL's case. It has everything I want in a conclusion and more!<br>• We get to see a different and a more in-depth side of some of our characters (ehem, my bby Holland *_*). However, I would have liked to know more about Lila and Kell's past since they're both still a mystery to me. <br>• Lots and lots and lots and lots of action (perhaps some deaths too?). Seriously, read it at your own risk ;)<br>• <b>RHY RHY RHY RHY RHY.</b><br>• <b>HOLLAND HOLLAND HOLLAND HOLLAND HOLLAND.</b><br>• Lila is even more reckless in this one but damn I still love her<br>• Kell and Alucard are such cutie pies. I live for their bickering :')<br>• Secondary characters that will make you fall in love and cry. <br>• <u>Some more action.</u> How do you defeat the undefeatable, you may ask? Read this book to find out :)<br>• THE ending will leave you sighing for days (at least I hope it does). <b>I loved it.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452810465ra/17746972.gif" width="266" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>---<br><br>Lbr, I'm <i>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RhBgPXb0Dfdem8JeIxs4GbpBZBjHFMTP/C+GQCDumfFgCpCS4nXdWK7Il4Chn6mfOAe60XbE5R8ywlerXKR1/Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FgImJJZt+jk7oHRAhha0AIYxY1yK+T6Zdji375GQ2E4wGNaLAuwqlsvzIZ4EkiWGBHe9lTspH0m41WYE7do0Qg==')})
  }

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/44752519-a-conjuring-of-light">Quotes from A Conjuring of Light</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Anoshe was a word for strangers in the street, and lovers between meetings, for parents and children, friends and family. It softened the blow of leaving. Eased the strain of parting. A careful nod to the certainty of today, the mystery of tomorrow. When a friend left, with little chance of seeing home, they said anoshe. When a loved one was dying, they said anoshe. When corpses were burned, bodies given back to the earth and souls to the stream, those left grieving said anoshe.<br /><br />Anoshe brought solace. And hope. And the strength to let go.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/8270472-anoshe-was-a-word-for-strangers-in-the-street-and">636 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Love and loss,” he said, “are like a ship and the sea. They rise together. The more we love, the more we have to lose. But the only way to avoid loss is to avoid love. And what a sad world that would be.&rdquo;</span>
